<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">FOR</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">ANNUAL MEETING OF SHAREHOLDERS</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">TO BE HELD ON WEDNESDAY, JUNE 22, 2016</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">INFORMATION ABOUT THE ANNUAL MEETING</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">When and where is the annual meeting?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The 2016 annual meeting of shareholders of T Bancshares, Inc. (the &#8220;Company,&#8221; &#8220;T Bancshares,&#8221; &#8220;we,&#8221; and &#8220;us&#8221;) will be held on Wednesday, June 22, 2016, beginning at 5:30 p.m., local time, at the main office of T Bank, N.A., 16200 Dallas Parkway, Suite 190, Dallas, Texas 75248.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Why am I receiving these materials?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">We are furnishing our proxy materials to our shareholders in connection with the solicitation of proxies by the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors to be voted at the annual meeting.&#160; The Board of Directors asks that you vote on the matters listed in the Notice of Annual Meeting, which are more fully described in this proxy statement.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">What is a proxy?</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">A proxy is your legal designation of another person to vote the stock you own. If you designate someone as your proxy or proxy holder in a written document, that document also is called a proxy or a proxy card.&#160; Patrick Howard and Shari Jensen have been designated as proxies or proxy holders for the annual meeting.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Who is soliciting my proxy?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Our Board of Directors is sending you this proxy statement in connection with the solicitation of proxies for use at the 2016 annual meeting of the shareholders of T Bancshares.&#160; Certain of our directors, officers, employees, and agents may also solicit proxies on our behalf personally, by mail, telephone or otherwise.&#160; We will not pay our directors, officers or employees any extra compensation for participating in this solicitation.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Who will bear the costs of soliciting proxies for the annual meeting?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">We will bear the cost of soliciting proxies for the annual meeting.&#160; We will also reimburse brokerage firms and other custodians, nominees and fiduciaries for reasonable out-of-pocket expenses incurred by them in sending proxy materials to the beneficial owners of our shares of common stock.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">What is the purpose of the annual meeting?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">At the annual meeting, shareholders will act upon the following matters:</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">In addition, our management will report on the performance of T Bancshares during 2015 and respond to appropriate questions from shareholders.&#160; Except with respect to the procedural matters incident to the conduct of the meeting, we are not aware of any other business to be brought before the meeting.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Who is entitled to vote at the annual meeting?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Only shareholders of record as of the close of business on the record date, April 29, 2016, are entitled to receive notice of the annual meeting and to vote the shares of common stock that they held on that date at the annual meeting or any postponement or adjournment thereof.&#160; Each outstanding common share entitles its holder to cast one vote on each matter to be voted upon at the annual meeting.&#160; The total number of common shares outstanding on the record date and eligible to cast votes at the annual meeting is 4,037,907.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">How many shares must be present to hold the annual meeting?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">We must have a quorum to conduct any business at the annual meeting.&#160; The presence at the annual meeting, in person or by proxy, of the holders of a majority of the shares of common stock outstanding on the record date, or 2,018,954<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>shares, will constitute a quorum at the annual meeting.&#160; For purposes of determining a quorum, abstentions, withheld votes in the election of directors and broker non-votes will be included in the number of shares present.&#160; A broker non-vote occurs when shares held by a bank, broker or other nominee are not voted on a particular matter.&#160; See &#8220;How will my shares be voted if I do not provide my proxy?&#8221; below.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">How do I vote?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">You may vote your shares either in person at the annual meeting or by proxy whether or not you attend the annual meeting.&#160; Shares held in your name as the shareholder of record may be voted:</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">(1) in person at the annual meeting,</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">(2) via the Internet at www.proxyvote.com and following the instructions,</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">(3) by telephone by calling 1-800-690-6903 and following the instructions, or</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">(4) by completing, dating and promptly returning the enclosed proxy card.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">We encourage you to vote electronically or by telephone. Votes submitted via the Internet or by telephone must be received by 11:59 p.m. Eastern Time on June&#160;21, 2016.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Shareholders who hold shares through a bank, broker or other nominee (&#8220;street name shareholders&#8221;) who receive or request printed copies of the proxy materials should be provided with voting instruction cards by the institution that holds their shares. If you are a street name shareholder who has received or requested a printed copy of the proxy materials and have not received a voting instruction card from your bank, broker or other nominee, please contact the institution that holds your shares.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Street name shareholders may also be eligible to vote their shares over the Internet or by telephone by following the voting instructions provided by the bank, broker or other nominee that holds the shares, using either the Internet address or the toll-free telephone number provided on the voting instruction card (if the bank, broker or other nominee provides these voting methods). Otherwise, please complete, sign and date the voting instruction card and return it promptly.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Even if you plan to attend the annual meeting, we recommend that you also submit your proxy or voting instructions as described above so that your vote will be counted if you later decide not to attend the meeting.</div>

<div id="DSPFPageNumberArea" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font id="DSPFPageNumber" style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-STYLE: normal">2</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.1pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.1pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 14.9pt">How will my shares be voted if I do not specify a choice with respect to each proposal?</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 14.9pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 14.9pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">If you sign and submit your proxy but do not mark your voting preferences, the proxy holders will vote your shares </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000">FOR </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">the election of each of the nominees for director, </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000">FOR</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000"> the ratification of the selection of our independent registered public accounting firm, and </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000">FOR</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000"> the advisory, non-binding vote on compensation of named executive officers.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">How will my shares be voted if I do not provide my proxy?</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 38.5pt">If you own your shares as a registered holder, which means that your shares of our common stock are registered in your name, your shares will be voted only if you submit your vote over the Internet or by telephone or if you return a signed proxy card.&#160; Otherwise, your shares will not be represented at the annual meeting and will not count toward the quorum requirement, which is explained under &#8220;How many shares must be present to hold the annual meeting?&#8221; above, unless you attend the annual meeting to vote them in person.</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 38.5pt">If you are a street name shareholder, your bank, broker or other nominee may or may not vote your shares if you have not provided voting instructions to the bank, broker or other nominee. Whether the bank, broker or other nominee may vote your shares depends on the proposals before the annual meeting. Under the rules that govern brokers, when a proposal is a &#8220;routine&#8221; matter, banks, brokers and other nominees may vote your shares in their discretion on &#8220;routine matters.&#8221; The ratification of the appointment of Whitley Penn LLP as our independent registered public accounting firm is a routine matter for which banks, brokers and other nominees may vote on behalf of their clients if no voting instructions are provided.</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">
</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">
<div id="DSPFPageHeader"></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 38.5pt">Under the rules that govern brokers, when a proposal is not a &#8220;routine matter&#8221; and your bank, broker or other nominee has not received your voting instructions with respect to that proposal, your bank, broker or other nominee cannot vote your shares on that proposal. This is called a &#8220;broker non-vote.&#8221; The election of the director nominees to the Board of Directors and the advisory vote on compensation paid to our named executive officers are not routine matters and, if your bank, broker or other nominee has not received your voting instructions with respect to these proposals, your bank, broker or other nominee cannot vote your shares on these proposals.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 38.5pt">&#160;</div>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 38.5pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">Your Participation in Voting the Shares You Own is Important. </font>Voting your shares is important to ensure that you have a say in the governance of the Company. Please review the proxy materials and follow the relevant instructions to vote your shares. We hope you will exercise your rights and fully participate as a shareholder.</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Can I change my vote?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">Yes.&#160; Even after you have submitted your proxy, you may change your vote at any time before the </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">annual meeting</font> is called to order<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">.&#160; If you are the shareholder of record, you may change your vote by </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">voting via </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">the Internet </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">or by telephone</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">, by timely mailing a new proxy bearing a later date (which automatically revokes the earlier proxy) </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">or by providing a written notice of revocation to our Corporate Secretary prior to the annual meeting being called to order.&#160; Mere attendance at the annual meeting is not sufficient to revoke a proxy.&#160; Attendance at the meeting will not cause your previously granted proxy to be revoked unless you specifically so request prior to the annual meeting being duly called to order.&#160; For shares you hold beneficially in street name, you may change your vote by submitting new voting instructions to your </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">bank, broker or nominee, or, if you have obtained a legal proxy from your </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">bank, broker or nominee giving you the right to vote your shares, by attending the meeting and voting in person.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">What vote is required to approve the proposals?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">In the election of directors, you may vote &#8220;FOR&#8221; all of the nominees, &#8220;WITHHOLD&#8221; for all of the nominees or &#8220;FOR ALL EXCEPT&#8221; and designate one or more of the nominees for whom you are withholding your vote.&#160; </font>Each director is required to be elected by a plurality of the votes cast at the annual meeting.&#160; If your vote is withheld with respect to any nominee, it will have no effect on the election of that nominee.</div>

<div id="DSPFPageBreakArea" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10pt; CLEAR: both; MARGIN-TOP: 10pt">
<div id="DSPFPageNumberArea" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font id="DSPFPageNumber" style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-STYLE: normal">3</font></div>

<div id="DSPFPageBreak" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
<hr style="BORDER-LEFT-WIDTH: 0px; HEIGHT: 2px; BORDER-RIGHT-WIDTH: 0px; BORDER-BOTTOM-WIDTH: 0px; COLOR: #000000; CLEAR: both; MARGIN: 4px 0px; BORDER-TOP-WIDTH: 0px; WIDTH: 100%; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #000000" noshade="noshade">
</div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.1pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.1pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">In the ratification of the selection of our independent registered public accounting firm, you may vote &#8220;FOR&#8221; the proposal, &#8220;AGAINST&#8221; the proposal, or &#8220;ABSTAIN&#8221; from voting on the proposal.&#160; The affirmative vote of a majority of the shares present in person or represented by proxy at the annual meeting and entitled to vote on this matter is required for ratification of the independent registered public accounting firm.&#160; If you abstain from voting on the proposal, it will have the same effect as a vote against the proposal.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">With respect to the advisory, non-binding vote on compensation of our named executive officers, you may vote &#8220;FOR&#8221; the proposal, &#8220;AGAINST&#8221; the proposal, or &#8220;ABSTAIN&#8221; from voting on the proposal. The affirmative vote of a majority of shares present in person or represented by proxy at the annual meeting and entitled to vote on this matter is required for approval of the compensation of our named executive officers. Voting for this proposal is being conducted on an advisory basis and, therefore, the voting results will not be binding on the Company, the Board or the compensation subcommittee. Abstentions will have the same effect as a vote against this proposal, whereas broker non-votes and shares not otherwise represented at the meeting will have no effect on the outcome of such matter.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Can I vote on other matters?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The matters presented at an annual meeting are limited to those properly presented by the Board of Directors and those properly presented by shareholders.&#160; We have not received notice from any shareholder as to any matter to come before the annual meeting.&#160; If any other matter is presented at the annual meeting, your signed proxy gives Patrick Howard and Shari Jensen, the proxy holders, authority to vote your shares.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">How does the Board of Directors recommend I vote on the proposals?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Our Board of Directors recommends a vote &#8220;FOR&#8221; the election of the nominated slate of directors, &#8220;FOR&#8221; the ratification of the selection of Whitley Penn LLP as our independent registered public accounting firm, and &#8220;FOR&#8221; the resolution approving the compensation of named executive officers. With respect to any other matter that properly comes before the meeting, the proxy holders will vote as recommended by our Board of Directors, or if no recommendation is given, in their own discretion.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Who can help answer my questions?</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">If you have any questions about the annual meeting or how to vote or revoke your proxy, or if you should need additional copies of this proxy statement or voting materials, please contact:</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">PROPOSAL ONE:<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><br>
</font> ELECTION OF DIRECTORS</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Nominees</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">Our bylaws authorize our Board of Directors to fix the number of directors at any number not less than one.&#160; Our Board currently consists </font>of 11 <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">members.&#160; You may not vote for a greater number of persons than the number of nominees named in this proxy statement</font>.<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">&#160; The nomination of these directors to stand for election at the </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">annual meeting has been recommended by the Nominating Subcommittee of the Executive Committee and approved by the Board of Directors.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">The Board of Directors has </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">presented the </font>11<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000"> nominees listed below for election as directors to serve until the 2017 annual meeting or until their successors are duly elected and qualified.&#160; All of the nominees listed below currently serve on our Board of Directors.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Unless otherwise specified in the accompanying form of proxy, proxies solicited hereby will be voted for the election of the nominees listed below.&#160; Each of the nominees has agreed to serve.&#160; If any of them should become unable to serve as a director, the Board of Directors may designate a substitute nominee.&#160; In that case, the proxies shall be voted for the substitute nominee or nominees to be designated by the Board of Directors.&#160; If no substitute nominees are available, the Board of Directors will act to reduce the number of directors.</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.1pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.1pt">
</div>

<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt"><font id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 1px; DISPLAY: inline-block; WIDTH: 36pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">Set forth below is certain information for each of the 11 nominees for election as directors at the annual meeting, including certain qualifications of each nominee considered by the Board of Directors in such nomination.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic">Stanley Allred</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">. </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">Mr. Allred has been a director of our Company since February 2003.&#160; Mr. Allred has spent the last 34 years in the securities industry, and he currently serves as Managing Partner for Allred Capital Management of Raymond James &amp; Associates where he is responsible for approximately $500 million in equity portfolios.&#160; He has extensive knowledge of the securities business and feels that his interaction with individuals who demand high quality banking services helps build T Bank, N.A.'s customer base. He also serves on the Executive Board of the Circle Ten Council, Boy Scouts of America, is a </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">director of the Baylor Oral Health Foundation and was a past Chairman for Dallas Heritage Village.&#160; He received his B.B.A. from Stephen F. Austin University. Mr. Allred holds several registration licenses with the </font>Financial Industry Regulatory Authority<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">.&#160; </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">We believe Mr. Allred brings </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">to the Board significant investment, financial planning, and financial skills important to the oversight of enterprise and operational risk management </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">of the </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">Company.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">Dan Basso</font>.<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160; </font>Mr. Basso has been a director of our Company since February 2003 and has served as Chairman since 2004.&#160; Mr. Basso is Chief Executive Officer of Systemware, Inc. and Systemware Professional Services, Inc., companies he co-founded in 1981.&#160; Systemware provides report distribution, document management and enterprise content management software and consulting services to a worldwide client base.&#160; He is also a partner in several real estate ventures.&#160; Before his involvement with Systemware, he held several technology and administrative positions with Frito-Lay, LTV Corporation and the Federal Reserve Bank of Dallas.&#160; Mr. Basso holds a Bachelor of Science degree in Aeronautical and Astronautical Engineering from the University of Illinois.&#160; Mr. Basso is the father of Frankie Basso, who is also one of our directors. We believe Mr. Basso&#8217;s experience and qualifications provide sound leadership to the Board, as well as strategic planning, significant corporate governance and operational risk management insight.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">Frankie Basso</font>.&#160; Mr. Basso has been a director of our Company since February 2003.&#160; Mr. Basso is the President&#160;and Chief Operating Officer&#160;of Systemware, Inc., where he has been employed since 1994. &#160;As Systemware's President and Chief Operating Officer, Frankie Basso is responsible for the day-to-day leadership of the company's sales, corporate marketing, development, support and services organizations. &#160;Mr. Basso is a life-long native of the Dallas area.&#160; He was born in Arlington, Texas, graduated from J. J. Pearce High School and earned a Bachelor of Arts degree in communications from Southern Methodist University.&#160; Frankie Basso is the son of Dan Basso, who is our Chairman. We believe Mr. Basso provides risk operations management, strategic planning, and marketing expertise to the Board, skills that are important as we continue to implement our business plan.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-STYLE: italic">David Carstens</font>.&#160; Mr. Carstens has been a director of our Company since February 2003.&#160; Mr. Carstens is a partner at Carstens &amp; Cahoon, L.L.P., a law firm that primarily represents clients seeking patents, trademarks, and copyrights. Mr. Carstens is a member of the Dallas Bar Association, has served as President of the Dallas/Ft. Worth Intellectual Property Law Association, and frequently speaks at continuing legal education seminars. Mr. Carstens has lived in the Dallas area for over 32 years.&#160; He holds a B.S. in Mechanical Engineering from Texas A&amp;M, a B.S. in Electrical Engineering from the University of Texas at Dallas, and a J.D. and M.B.A. from Southern Methodist University.&#160; We believe Mr. Carstens brings risk management, strategic planning, as well as corporate governance skills to the Board.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic">Ron Denheyer</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">.&#160; Mr. Denheyer has been a director of our Company since February 2003.&#160; In 1998, Mr. Denheyer joined Systemware, Inc., and is </font>Executive <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">Vice President and Chief Financial Officer.&#160; Prior to joining Systemware, Inc., he served as Division Controller of Argonaut Insurance Company.&#160; Mr. Denheyer is a member of Financial Executives International, a premier professional organizational for chief financial officers, controllers and cashiers.&#160; He currently sits on the Board of Trustees at Parish Episcopal School and serves as Chairman of the Endowment Board.&#160; He also sits on the Board of 1 Million 4 Anna Foundation.&#160; He is a graduate from James Martin High School in Arlington, Texas and holds a Bachelor of Arts degree from Texas Christian University and a Master of Business Administration from the University of Dallas. We believe Mr. Denheyer brings strong investment, accounting and financial skills important to the oversight of our financial reporting and operational risk management.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic">Patrick Howard</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">.</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">&#160; </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">Mr. Howard was named President &amp; Chief Executive Officer </font>of the Company&#160;<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">and T Bank, N.A. in July 2010. He joined</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #ff0000">&#160;</font>the Company&#160;<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">as a Director and Executive Vice President, Chief Operating Officer of T Bank, N.A. in September 2007. During his career, Mr. Howard has had executive level and direct managerial responsibility for numerous areas of bank operations including credit origination and administration, retail branch operations, mortgage servicing and loan operations, compliance, technology, investments, risk mitigation, internal controls development and implementation, and strategic planning. Mr. Howard started his banking career in 1986 in San Antonio, Texas. He is an honors graduate of the University of Texas at San Antonio where he earned a Bachelor of Business Administration degree in finance. We believe Mr. Howard provides the Board with sound leadership, strategic planning skills, as well as extensive understanding and experience in managing operational, credit, and regulatory risk and asset liability management.</font></div>

Prior to joining T Bank in 2004, he was Executive Vice President and Senior Lending Officer of First Independent National Bank in Plano, Texas. Between September 1987 and August 1997, he served in various lending officer capacities with Willow Bend National Bank, Bonham State Bank and Compass Bank before joining First State Bank of Texas (formerly Addison National Bank) in August 1997 as a Senior Vice President and Loan Officer.&#160; Mr. Jones served in these capacities for approximately three years before leaving the bank to become an Executive Vice President and Senior Lending Officer of First Independent National Bank where he served until April 2004. <div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Corporate Governance</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Corporate Governance Principles and Board Matters</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Board Independence</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Our Board of Directors has determined that Messrs. Allred, Dan Basso, Frankie Basso, Carstens, Denheyer, Langford, Mapes, McDougal and Youngblood are &#8220;independent&#8221; directors under the applicable NASDAQ rules.&#160; Mr. Howard currently serves as our President and Chief Executive Officer and Mr. Jones currently serves as our Plano Market President.&#160; Accordingly, they are not deemed to be &#8220;independent&#8221; directors under the applicable NASDAQ rules.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Director Qualifications</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">We believe that our directors should have the highest professional and personal ethics and values.&#160; They should have broad experience at the policy-making level in business, government or banking.&#160; They should be committed to enhancing shareholder value and should have sufficient time to carry out their duties and to provide insight and practical wisdom based on experience.&#160; Their service on other boards of public companies should be limited to a number that permits them, given their individual circumstances, to perform responsibly all director duties for us.&#160; Each director must represent the interests of all shareholders.&#160; When considering potential director candidates, the Board also considers the candidate&#8217;s character, judgment, diversity, age, skills, including financial literacy and experience in the context of our needs and the needs of the Board of Directors. Our Board of Directors has no formal policy with regard to the consideration of diversity in identifying director nominees, but the board of directors believes that the backgrounds and qualifications of the directors, considered as a group, should provide a significant composite mix of experience, knowledge and abilities that will allow the board of directors to fulfill its responsibilities.&#160; Nominees are not discriminated against on the basis of race, religion, national origin, sexual orientation, disability or any other basis proscribed by law.&#160; For more information, see &#8220;Nominating Subcommittee of the Executive Committee&#8221; beginning on page 11.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Shareholder Communications with Our Board of Directors</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Our Board of Directors has established a process for shareholders to communicate with the Board of Directors or with individual directors.&#160; Shareholders who wish to communicate with our Board of Directors or with individual directors should direct written correspondence to our Corporate Secretary at our principal executive offices located at 16200 Dallas Parkway, Suite 190, Dallas, Texas 75248.<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160; </font>Any such communication must contain:</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Board Meetings</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Our Board of Directors convenes monthly and calls special meetings as circumstances may require.&#160; The Board of Directors met 14 times in 2015.&#160; Each director attended at least 79% of the total number of meetings of the Board of Directors and the Board committees of T Bancshares and T Bank, N.A. of which he or she was a member during 2015.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">We do not have a policy that requires directors to attend our annual meeting of shareholders.&#160; At our 2015 annual meeting of shareholders, nine directors were in attendance.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Board Leadership Structure</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">The roles of Chairman and Chief Executive Officer are separate positions within the Company.&#160; Mr. Dan Basso serves as our Chairman, and Mr. Howard serves as our Chief Executive Officer.&#160; We separate the roles of Chairman and Chief Executive Officer in recognition of the differences between the two roles.&#160; The Chief Executive Officer is responsible for setting the strategic direction for the </font>Company and our subsidiary <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">bank and the day to day leadership and performance of the Company, while the Chairman of the Board provides guidance to the Chief Executive Officer and presides over meetings of the Board of Directors.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Risk Oversight</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">The Board of Directors has an active role, as a whole and also at the committee level, in overseeing </font>risk<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 3px double; COLOR: #0000ff">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">management</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">.&#160; The Board of Directors regularly receives reports from senior management on areas of material risk to the bank, including our credit, liquidity, operational and legal and regulatory risks.&#160; Pursuant to its charter, the Audit Committee reviews our major financial risk exposures and the steps management has taken to monitor and control such exposures, and it also meets periodically with management to discuss policies with respect to risk assessment and risk management.&#160; In addition, the compensation subcommittee of the Executive Committee oversees the management of risks relating to our executive and non-executive compensation plans and arrangements, and the nominating subcommittee of the Executive Committee manages risks associated with the independence of the Board of Directors and potential conflicts of interest.&#160; While each committee oversees certain risks and the management of such risks, the entire Board of Directors is regularly informed through committee reports about such risks.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Code of Conduct</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">We are committed to having sound corporate governance principles, both at the holding company level and at T Bank, N.A., our subsidiary bank.&#160; Such principles are essential to running our business efficiently and to maintaining our integrity in the marketplace.&#160; We have adopted a Code of Conduct and Conflicts of Interest Policy, which, together with the policies referred to therein, is applicable to all our directors, officers and employees.&#160; The Code of Conduct and Conflicts of Interest Policy covers all areas of professional conduct and ethics, including conflicts of interest, disclosure obligations, insider trading and confidential information, as well as compliance with all laws, rules and regulations applicable to our business. We strongly encourage all employees, officers and directors to promptly report any violations of any of our policies.&#160; A copy of our Code of Conduct and Conflicts of Interest Policy is posted to the Company&#8217;s website under &#8220;About Us-Investor Relations.&#8221; The policy may also be obtained by any person, without charge, upon written request to T Bancshares, Inc., Attn: Corporate Secretary, 16200 Dallas Parkway, Suite 190, Dallas, Texas 75248.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 1px; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; WIDTH: 36pt"></div>

<div>&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Director Compensation</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Meetings of our Board of Directors are held regularly each month.&#160; Until January 1, 2015, the Company did not compensate directors for any service provided as a director.&#160; Beginning in 2015, non-employee directors are compensated in accordance with the 2014 Non-employee Directors&#8217; Common Stock Plan. Under the plan, non-employee directors are awarded annually after the annual meeting of shareholders a number of common shares based upon the director&#8217;s actual participation in regular and special meetings of the Board of Directors, as well as committees thereof.&#160; Directors will be awarded 100 common shares for each regular board meeting attended and 25 common shares for each board committee or special board meeting attended during the preceding 12 months. Mr. Howard and Mr. Jones, as employee directors, are not eligible to participate in the plan.</div>

<div style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Committees of T Bancshares and T Bank, N.A.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Our Board of Directors has an Audit Committee and Executive Committee (with compensation and nominating subcommittees). The Audit Committee meets quarterly or as necessary and the Executive Committee meets as circumstances require. The Board of Directors of T Bank, N.A. also has a number of committees, including an Audit Committee, an Asset &amp; Liability Committee, Loan Committee, Trust Committee, Executive Committee (with compensation and nominating subcommittees) and a Technology Committee, that meet quarterly or as circumstances require.&#160; The membership during the last fiscal year and the function of each of the committees are described below.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Audit Committee</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Our Board of Directors established the Audit Committee to assist the Board in fulfilling its responsibilities for general oversight of the integrity of our consolidated financial statements, compliance with legal and regulatory requirements, the independent auditors&#8217; qualifications and independence, the performance of independent auditors and our internal audit function, and risk assessment and risk management. The duties of the Audit Committee include:</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div id="DSPFPageBreak" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
<hr style="BORDER-LEFT-WIDTH: 0px; HEIGHT: 2px; BORDER-RIGHT-WIDTH: 0px; BORDER-BOTTOM-WIDTH: 0px; COLOR: #000000; CLEAR: both; MARGIN: 4px 0px; BORDER-TOP-WIDTH: 0px; WIDTH: 100%; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #000000" noshade="noshade">
</div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.1pt"><br style="LINE-HEIGHT: 13.1pt">
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">The members of the Audit Committee are David Carstens, Ron Denheyer, Charles Mapes</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">,</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000"> Thomas McDougal</font>, and Frankie Basso<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">. </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">Mr. Carstens serves as Chairmen of the Audit Committee.&#160; The Audit Committee held four meetings during fiscal year 2015.&#160; The Board of Directors has determined that each member of the Audit Committee is &#8220;independent&#8221; according to the rules and regulations of the Securities and Exchange Commission (&#8220;SEC&#8221;) and </font>NASDAQ.&#160; <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">In addition, the Board has determined that each member of the Audit Committee is &#8220;financially literate&#8221; under the current listing standards of NASDAQ.&#160; The Board has also determined that Mr.&#160;Denheyer is an &#8220;audit committee financial expert&#8221; as defined by the SEC rules.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">Our Board of Directors has adopted a written charter for the Audit Committee.&#160; A copy of our Audit Committee Charter is available on the &#8220;About Us-Investor Relations&#8221; page of the Bank&#8217;s website at </font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #0000ff"><u>www.tbank.com</u></font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000">.</font></div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt">Executive Committee</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The Executive Committee meets as needed and, with certain exceptions, has the same powers as the Board of Directors in the management of the business affairs of T Bancshares between meetings of our full Board of Directors.&#160; The Board of Directors, from time to time, charges the Executive Committee with specific responsibilities and tasks as it deems appropriate.&#160; The Committee is not intended to act in place of the full board, but rather in a support role.&#160; The Committee makes recommendations to the Board of Directors regarding matters important to the overall management and strategic operation of T Bancshares and T Bank, N.A.&#160; The members of the Executive Committee are Dan Basso (Chairman), Chuck Mapes, David Carstens, and Patrick Howard. Mr. Basso serves as Chairman of the Executive Committee.&#160; The Executive Committee held two meetings during the 2015 fiscal year.&#160; The Executive Committee has a compensation subcommittee and a nominating subcommittee.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt">Compensation Subcommittee of the Executive Committee</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The compensation subcommittee of the Executive Committee recommends to the Board of Directors the compensation of executive personnel, compensation paid to directors and the policies, terms and conditions of employment of all employees of T Bancshares.&#160; The compensation subcommittee does not operate according to a written charter.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Each member of the Executive Committee is also a member of the compensation subcommittee with the exception of committee members who are also executive officers of the Company or T Bank, N.A.&#160; None of our executive officers who are also directors participate in compensation subcommittee deliberations regarding their own compensation.&#160; The compensation subcommittee held one meeting during the fiscal year 2015.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The compensation subcommittee approves all new executive officer hires, incentive compensation arrangements, bonuses, employment agreements, and executive officer salary increases. The subcommittee has the authority to establish compensation for executive officers. It considers experience, qualifications, and employment market conditions in establishing compensation levels. Executive officers may provide information and recommendations to the subcommittee for consideration except when it pertains to their own compensation or employment arrangements. The subcommittee refers to industry publications and salary surveys to assist in determining compensation levels of executive officers of similarly situated financial institutions based on geographic location, size, and complexity as compared to the Company. The subcommittee has not utilized outside consultants to establish compensation levels, but does not rule out such utilization in the future and has the authority to do so.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt">Nominating Subcommittee of the Executive Committee</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The nominating subcommittee of the Executive Committee reviews all Board-recommended and shareholder- recommended director nominees, determining each nominee&#8217;s qualifications and making a recommendation to the full Board as to which persons should be our Board&#8217;s nominees.&#160; Each member of the Executive Committee is also a member of the nominating subcommittee.&#160; The nominating subcommittee held one meeting during the fiscal year 2015.&#160; The duties and responsibilities of the nominating subcommittee include:</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

Our nominating subcommittee utilizes a variety of methods for identifying and evaluating nominees for director.&#160; Our nominating subcommittee will regularly assess the appropriate size of the Board and whether any vacancies on the Board are expected due to retirement or other circumstances.&#160; When considering potential director candidates, the nominating subcommittee has certain criteria that it views as relevant and is likely to consider.&#160; These criteria include, but are not limited to, a candidate&#8217;s:</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Candidates&#8217; character, judgment, skills, including financial literacy, and experience in the context of our needs, the needs of T Bank, N.A. and the existing directors are additional factors considered by the subcommittee. The subcommittee does not assign a particular weight to these individual factors. Similarly, the nominating subcommittee does not expect any individual candidate to meet all, or even more than a few, of these factors. Instead, the nominating subcommittee looks for a mix of factors that, when combined with the experience and credentials of other candidates and existing directors, will provide the Company and its shareholders with a diverse and experienced Board. To date, all director nominees have been identified by current directors or management based on personal acquaintance or reputation. The Company has never engaged a third party to identify director candidates, and the Company has never received a proposed director candidate from a source outside the Company, including its shareholders.&#160; However, the Board would consider any director candidate proposed in good faith by a shareholder of the Company. Our Board of Directors has established a procedure whereby our shareholders can nominate potential director candidates.&#160; See &#8220;Shareholder Proposals for the Next Annual Meeting of Shareholders&#8221; beginning on page 23.&#160; The nominating subcommittee will consider director candidates recommended by our shareholders in a similar manner as those recommended by members of management or other directors, provided the shareholder submitting such nomination has complied with procedures set forth in our bylaws.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; COLOR: #000000; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Other than Dan Basso, our Chairman of the board who serves on our nominating subcommittee of the Executive Committee, no candidate for election to our Board has been recommended within the preceding year by a beneficial owner of 5% or more of our common stock.</div>
